/**
 * Remove the gray background color from active links in IE 10.
 */
a {
	color: #b30404;
	text-decoration: none;
  	background: transparent; }

/**
 * Address `outline` inconsistency between Chrome and other browsers.
 */
a:focus {
  outline: thin dotted; }

/**
 * Improve readability when focused and also mouse hovered in all browsers.
 */
a:active,
a:hover {
	color: #ff0000;
	text-decoration: none;
 	outline: 0; 
	transition: all ease-in-out .1s;
	}

.thePost a {
	
}

	.thePost a:hover {
		text-decoration: underline;	
	}

.news-basket article h2 a, .content article h2 a {
	color: #231e1e;	
}

.news-basket article h2 a:hover, .content article h2 a:hover {
	color: #ff3300;
	text-decoration: underline;
}

                                    <div class="wrapper">
                                        <h2><a href="http://asus.adrenaline.uol.com.br/2017/03/21/48871/na-compra-de-placas-de-video-asus-gtx-ganhe-for-honor-ou-ghost-recon-wildlands-/">Na compra de placas de vídeo ASUS GTX ganhe For Honor ou Ghost Recon: Wildlands </a></h2>
                                        <div class="author">
                                            <p>21/03/2017 10:59                                            <span class="noComm">
                                                <span class="tip tip-down"></span>
                                                <span class="disqus-comment-count" data-disqus-identifier="48871"></span>
                                            </span>
                                            </p>

					newNav.append('<div class="back-to-top" style="margin-top:7px;"><span class="icon-adr-trianguloflat-top"></span></div>');
					
					newNav.find('.back-to-top').click(function(e){
						$("html, body").animate({scrollTop:0}, 500, 'easeInOutCirc');
					});
					
					newNav.css({'position': 'fixed', 'top': -50, 'z-index': 50000, 'width': 1020});
					newNav.animate({'top': 0}, 500, 'easeInOutCirc');
					
				} else if($(window).scrollTop() < distancia_menu_template_2_show && $('.fixed-nav').length > 0) {
					
					newNav.removeClass('fixed-nav');
					
					newNav.css({'position': 'relative', 'top': '', 'z-index': '', 'width': ''});
					
										newNav.find('.menu').css('margin-top', '25px');
										newNav.find('#busca-topo').css('margin-top', '18px');
			
					newNav.find('#logo-topo').css('display', '');
					newNav.find('.secoes').css('display', '');
					newNav.find('.destaque').css('display', '');
					newNav.find('.social').css('display', '');
					newNav.find('.userLink').css('display', '');
					
					newNav.find('.adrenaline-small-logo').remove();
					newNav.find('#social-roll').remove();
					newNav.find('.search-button').remove();
					newNav.find('.back-to-top').remove();
					
					if(newNavInterna){
						newNav.find('.secoes-interna').remove();
					}
				}
				
			});

			$(window).resize(function(e) {

				if ($("#mascara_hl1").length) {
					if($(document).width()>1023) { 
						$('#mascara_hl1').css({'height': '400px'});
					} else {
						var img_hl1_w = $('#img_hl1').width();
						var img_hl1_h = $('#img_hl1').height();
						console.log("[W:"+img_hl1_w+"] [H:"+img_hl1_h+"]");
						$('#mascara_hl1').css({'height': ''+img_hl1_h+'px'});
					}
				}
				
				
			});

			$(document).on('mouseover', '.zoomImg', function(event) {
				var o = $(this);
				var s = o.prev('span.jzoom-icon');
				if (s.length) s.show();
			}).on('mouseout', '.zoomImg', function(event) {
				var o = $(this);
				var s = o.prev('span.jzoom-icon');
				if (s.length) s.hide();
			});
	
			$(".thePost, .video_chamada").fitVids();
	
			$('.thePost div.content').find('img').each(function(ix, el) {
				$(el).ready(function() {
					$('<img/>')
						.attr('src', $(el).attr('src'))
						.load(function() {
							if($(el).parent().hasClass( "fancybox" )) { } else {
								$(el).css('height', 'auto');
							}
						});
				});
			});
	
			$('.thePost div.postContent').find('img').each(function(ix, el) {
				$(el).ready(function() {
					$('<img/>')
						.attr('src', $(el).attr('src'))
						.load(function() {
							if($(el).parent().hasClass( "fancybox" )) { } else {
								$(el).css('height', 'auto');
							}
						});
				});
			});
